SCRIPT ORIGINAL:

def search(table, x, y, depth, max_depth):

    if depth == max_depth:
        return True

    if x < 0 or x >= 10 or y < 0 or y >= 10:
        return False

    if depth >= 0 and table[x][y][depth] == 0:
        return False

    if search(table, x-2, y-1, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True
    if search(table, x-2, y, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True
    if search(table, x-2, y+1, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True

    if search(table, x-1, y-2, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True
    if search(table, x, y-2, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True
    if search(table, x+1, y-2, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True

    if search(table, x+2, y-1, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True
    if search(table, x+2, y, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True
    if search(table, x+2, y+1, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True

    if search(table, x-1, y+2, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True
    if search(table, x, y+2, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True
    if search(table, x+1, y+2, depth+1, max_depth):
        return True

while True:
    px,py = [int(i) for i in input().split()]
    if px == 0 and py == 0:
        break

    table = [[[0 for i in range(10)] for j in range(10)] for k in range(10)]

    n = int(input())
    N = [int(i) for i in input().split()]
    traps = []

    for i in range(0, len(N), 2):
        x = N[i]
        y = N[i+1]
        prx = max(x-1, 0)
        pry = max(y-1, 0)
        pox = min(x+1, 9)
        poy = min(y+1, 9)

        d = int(i//2)
        table[prx][pry][d] = 1
        table[prx][y][d] = 1
        table[prx][poy][d] = 1
        table[x][pry][d] = 1
        table[x][y][d] = 1
        table[x][poy][d] = 1
        table[pox][pry][d] = 1
        table[pox][y][d] = 1
        table[pox][poy][d] = 1

    if search(table, px, py, -1, n):
        print("OK")
    else:
        print("NA")
